agali subah main rishikesh pahunchaa
 
 
 i took a dip in the Ganges
 
 
 ganga wo nadi jiskaa naam maine itnaa suna tha lekin pehali baar use dekh rahaa tha uskaa anubhav kar rahaa tha
 
 
 i was told about the Sivananda Ashram of Rishikesh
 
 
 main vahaan gaya
 
 
 As i entered the ashram, i felt a strange wave that brought relief to my restless soul
 
 
 chaaron ore sadhu baithe hue the dhyaan main tallin
 
 
 i felt that someone would answer the questions bothering me, calm my worries
 
 
 mujhe swami shivanand se milane kaa mauka mila
 
 
 He did not mind my being a Muslim
 
 
 balki isse pehle ki main kuch bolta unhone mujhase meri chintaa ke bare main puch liya
 
 
 i was surprised how they realized my trouble
 
 
 unhone kaha tumhaara muskabil air force kaa payalat bananaa nahin he
 
 
 What you want to become is already decided
 lekin kuch banane ke baad bhi unka yah adhuraa sapana peechha karata rahaa
 Even after becoming President, he persecuted that the pilot could not be made
 jaipur litarechar festival main unhone is dard ko saajha karte hue bataaya ki 2005 main jab main raashtrapati tha to vayusena pramukh mere paas aae
 i told him that i could never fulfill my dream of becoming a pilot, the Air Force chief told me to take a little training and then i finally flew for forty minutes in April 2007 from Lohegaon Air Force Base in Pune to Sukhoi 30 MKI fighter aircraft
 ye kisi bhi raashtrapati kii pehali udaan thi
 This flight changed the office and stature of the President forever in the eyes of the soldiers and the army
 apane commander ko akaash main morcha sambhalate dekh kis jawan kaa hausala nahin badha hoga
 The journey of his life started from 1931
 dwitiya vishwayuddh ke asar ko unhone apane rameswaram main bhi jhela or yaad kiya
 In the last few years, his close aide Sreejan Pal Singh has mentioned the last things on his Facebook page
 saadhe gyaarah baje kalam sahab kaa antim twit aata he ki main ai iem shilong ja rahaa hum
 To deliver a lecture on the topic Creating a Livable Planet Earth
 is twit ke baad baarah baje kalam sahab guwahati jane ke liye vimaan se ravaanaa hote hai

 dhai ghante kii yatra ke dauraan kai baar vimaan ne monsooni badalon ke bich hichkole bhi khaaye
 It was a normal thing for him
 unhone hilte hue jahaaz main jab bhi mujhe daraa hua dekha, khidki ke parde hataae or baahar dekhte hue kaha ki ab tumhen dar nahin lagegaa
 Srijan writes that after this, for two and a half hours we left by road to IIM Shillong
 paanch ghante ke dauraan wo mujhase baaten karte rahe, charchaa karte rahe
 It was the last of hundreds of aircraft and road trips made with him in the last six years, every visit was special
 aakiri daure main doctor kalam punjab main aatankwaadi hamale ko lekar kaafii chintit dikhe
 He was saddened by the death of innocent people
 im shilong main unhen Creating a Livable Planet Earth vishay par vyaakhyaan dena tha
 Linking the incident of Punjab to the subject, he said that it seems like man-made forces have become a greater threat to the earth, just like pollution
 iske baad hamane hinsa, pradooshan or prakruti main insaani dakhal par baatcheet kii or kaha ki aise main to dharti rahane laayak nahin rah jaaegi
 He said that maybe in the next thirty years, the earth will be in such a bad condition, so you people will have to do something for it immediately
 unki antim chintaaon main yah baat bhi shaamil thi ki sansad main kaise gatirodh khatm ho

 baat ho

 doctor maanas bihari verma ne jab khabar main suni to khud ko kamare main band kar liya
 After retirement, Dr
 Verma returned to Darbhanga at the behest of APJ Abdul Kalam and started working to spread science in the schools there
 kalam ke kehane par hi doctor verma viksit bharat foundation ke liye kaam karne lage
 Three mobile science labs and six instructors have reached 250 schools in Darbhanga, Madhubani
 12500 chaatro kaa vigyaan se rishta joda he

 raashtrapati rahete hue bhi disbanr 2005 main lalit narayan mithila vishvavidhyalay ke dikshant samaaroh main hissaa liya
 In the 90s, Doctor Verma and Doctor Kalam came close to each other when building a light combo aircraft at the Aeronautic Development Agency in Bengaluru
 doctor kamaal ke nirdesan main hi verma ne tejas aircraft banaaya

 ek din unhen phone aata he ki raashtrapati apije abdul kalam kerala ke daure par aa rahe hai or unase milane kii khwaahish rakhte hai

 ve payalat bananaa chaahate the

 Kalam Saheb, who came out to show the world dreams, also had an unfulfilled dream
 ve payalat bananaa chaahate the

 ye kisi bhi raashtrapati kii pehali udaan thi

 dharmik kaaryakramon kaa bhi aayojan hota he

 kya he radhashtami kii kathisaki kai manyataayen hai
